# Chiral I Strengthening PDF: Obligation Ledger

Source: `/Users/raeez/Desktop/corrections/chiral1 Research Paper Strengthening.pdf`.
Extraction date: 2026-06-05.

This note records the load-bearing mathematical obligations from the
strengthening memo. It is not a replacement for the manuscript; it is a
repair queue for theorem surfaces that must not silently overclaim.

## Fatal Gaps

1. **Signed log-FM cooperad.**  The relative logarithmic
   Fulton--MacPherson cooperad is the keystone.  Mok supplies the
   geometry of strata, codimensions, tropical cones, and degeneration
   correspondences.  The manuscript must separately supply rational
   chain models, Gysin residues, determinant-line signs, proper
   pushforwards, finite stabilizer normalisations, and homotopy-coherent
   cocompositions.  Any ambient \(D_{\mathrm{mod}}^{\log\,2}=0\)
   statement is conditional until this package is invoked.

2. **Five-object firewall.**  The objects
   \(A\), \(B_X(A)\), \(A^{\mathrm i}=H^\bullet B_X(A)\),
   \(A^!\), and \(Z_{\mathrm{ch}}^{\mathrm{der}}(A)\) live in different
   ambients.  No theorem may identify two of them without naming the
   functor and hypothesis package.

3. **Theorem B completion.**  Raw direct-sum bar--cobar inversion is
   false in class \(\mathsf M\).  Valid forms are finite-window
   conilpotent statements or strict Mittag--Leffler completed
   coderived/contraderived statements.

4. **Class \(\mathsf M\) as test case.**  Virasoro and \(W\)-families
   must be used to justify the completed formalism, not treated as a
   minor exception.

5. **\(H_{\Delta_5}\) recognition.**  The Hall--Borcherds/K3
   equivalence is a target until the finite-window Hall source,
   parity/root fixtures, PBW/no-extra-root condition, completion maps,
   and comparison morphisms are constructed.

6. **Theorem H hypotheses.**  Chiral Hochschild amplitude \([0,2]\)
   requires PBW chiral Koszulness, completion, finite-type/perfectness,
   genericity, strict Mittag--Leffler passage, and the PBW/Arnold
   contraction.  Outside that package the defect complex
   \(K^\bullet_{\mathrm{DH}}(A)\) must be named.

## Current Repair Lane

The first pass repairs the log-FM \(D^2\) grammar:

- fixed smooth-curve/convolution \(D^2=0\) remains unconditional;
- relative ambient \(D_{\mathrm{mod}}^{\log\,2}=0\) is conditional on
  the signed log-FM residue-pushforward package;
- compute/test oracle text must preserve this distinction.

The second pass repairs the five-object firewall:

- bar cohomology is written first as the coalgebra
  \(A^{\mathrm i}=H^\bullet B_X(A)\);
- \(A^!\) is reached only through the separate Verdier/continuous-linear
  dual branch with finite-type or completed convergence hypotheses;
- \(Z_{\mathrm{ch}}^{\mathrm{der}}(A)\) remains the Hochschild-cochain
  bulk object and is never identified with \(B_X(A)\) or \(A^!\);
- enumerative tables may compare \(\dim A^{\mathrm i}\) with
  \(\dim A^!\), but only as a Hilbert-function statement after the dual
  branch exists.

The third pass repairs Theorem B completion surfaces:

- a boolean such as `bar_cobar_inversion=True` or `exact_recovery=True`
  is insufficient unless accompanied by the ambient carrying the counit;
- class \(\mathsf M\) \textup{(}Virasoro, principal \(W_N\),
  \(W_\infty\)\textup{)} is the test case, not an exception: raw
  direct-sum chain recovery is false there;
- valid class-\(\mathsf M\) recovery is finite-window strict
  Mittag--Leffler or weight-completed pro-conilpotent/coderived;
- raw \(\Omega B(A)\to A\) is allowed only on the finite-window
  conilpotent surface with the (H3b) comparison hypotheses.

The fourth pass repairs Theorem H hypothesis surfaces:

- chiral Hochschild amplitude \([0,2]\) is stated only on the
  PBW chiral Koszul, finite-type/perfect, generic,
  \(E_\infty\)-completed, strict Mittag--Leffler surface;
- the PBW/Arnold Shelton--Yuzvinsky contraction is named as the
  collision-depth collapse mechanism, not replaced by bare
  Fulton--MacPherson formality;
- off that package the high-degree object is the Hochschild
  Koszul-defect complex
  \(\mathrm{KD}_{\mathrm H}^{\bullet}(A)\), with concentration allowed
  only after its relevant high-degree cohomology is proved zero;
- executable model surfaces return or test an explicit Theorem H
  scope record, and K7 in the holographic-code dictionary is
  conditional on the Theorem H package rather than unconditional.

The fifth pass repairs \(H_{\Delta_5}\) recognition surfaces:

- scalar evidence from \(\phi_{0,1}^{K3}\), the Borcherds/Gritsenko
  product, \(\Delta_5\)-weight \(5\), and low-level root-multiplicity
  checks is separated from the chain-level Hall--Borcherds/K3
  recognition theorem;
- no shadow-tower, sewing, or scalar product-formula computation may
  assert \(\exp(-\Theta_A)=\) the BKM denominator as a chain-level
  equality;
- recognition remains conditional until the four-part datum
  \((\beta,\delta,\varepsilon,\tau)\) is supplied: finite-window
  \(E_1\)-chiral Hall bialgebra morphism, completed Drinfeld-double
  extension, current-envelope morphism along the elliptic fibre, and
  derived-centre trace identity;
- each executable K3/Delta5 bridge surface must report
  `recognition_complete=False` unless it also records the finite
  Hall/CoHA source, parity/root fixtures, PBW/no-extra-root condition,
  nondegenerate Hall pairing/radical quotient, current locality,
  \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\) commutation, strict
  Mittag--Leffler completion maps, and comparison morphisms to
  \(\mathbf H_{\Delta_5}\).

The sixth pass repairs MC5 status surfaces:

- MC5 is not a single Boolean theorem status.  The analytic
  HS-sewing lane, the coderived BV/bar quasi-isomorphism, and the
  strict Mittag--Leffler completed/pro/\(J\)-adic chain surface are
  proved on their stated ambients;
- the bounded direct-sum chain ambient fails in class \(\mathsf M\);
- the genus-\(0\) moduli-integration amplitude pairing is conditional,
  and the physical BV/BRST, Feynman, AGT, and holographic comparison
  surfaces remain downstream of the proved algebraic packet;
- executable concordance audits must therefore accept
  `MC_STATUS["MC5"] == "PARTIALLY_PROVED"` only when accompanied by an
  ambient-split status record separating proved, failing, conditional,
  and downstream-open surfaces.

The seventh pass repairs the open/closed comparison firewall:

- \(Z_{\mathrm{ch}}^{\mathrm{der}}(A)\) is the universal algebraic
  closed actor of the boundary \(A_\infty\)-chiral algebra, not the
  physical factorization algebra
  \(\operatorname{Obs}^{\mathrm{bulk}}(T)\) of an HT theory;
- the symbol "bulk" is reserved for the physical object unless the
  text explicitly says algebraic closed sector or intrinsic categorical
  center;
- a physical-bulk identification requires OCA data: boundary
  identification, local-operator shadow, continuous brace map,
  quasi-isomorphism, and completion;
- \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\) records a typed
  closed-to-open action on \((Z_{\mathrm{ch}}^{\mathrm{der}}(A),A)\);
  it does not make the bar complex itself an
  \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\) bulk object.
- QEC, HaPPY, toric-code, and tensor-network comparisons are algebraic
  analogies or shadow-amplitude checks until an OCA comparison theorem
  identifies a physical bulk factorization algebra.

The eighth pass repairs ordered-to-symmetric averaging surfaces:

- scalar/profile projection statements such as
  \(\operatorname{av}(K_A^{E_1})=K_A\) are not automatically chain-map
  theorems;
- averaging commutes with the ordered bar differential and preserves
  the convolution bracket only after the \(R\)-twisted
  \(\Sigma_n\)-descent package is supplied: \(R\)-twisted descent,
  differential equivariance, bracket equivariance, continuous Reynolds
  operator, and completed finite arity windows;
- degree-\(2\) \(\kappa\)-averaging checks are scalar shadows.  They do
  not prove that the full ordered bar differential descends;
- naive Reynolds quotienting is not the chain map in the pole-valued
  chiral setting.  The descended symmetric bar uses the
  \(R\)-twisted local-system quotient and the factorization coproduct.

The ninth pass repairs Theorem C / Lagrangian-complementarity
surfaces:

- Theorem C is a three-layer statement: C0 fiber-center identification,
  C1 scalar/Verdier eigenspace complementarity, and C2
  shifted-symplectic Lagrangian upgrade;
- scalar checks of \(\kappa(A)+\kappa(A^!)\), \(F_g(A)+F_g(A^!)\),
  and rank-one scalar Gram matrices are C0/C1 indicators only;
- C2 requires an explicit hypothesis package: C0 fiber-center
  identification, C1 homotopy eigenspace decomposition,
  uniform-weight perfectness, nondegenerate cyclic pairing, finite
  modular envelope, closed cyclic pairing, skew-adjoint differential,
  modular bracket compatibility, twisted-tensor acyclicity, and
  ambient BV/QME input;
- executable Lagrangian helpers must return the C2 missing-hypothesis
  list.  A boolean such as `is_lagrangian=True` is valid only when that
  list is empty; otherwise the helper may report only scalar
  complementarity support.

The tenth pass repairs Theorem D / genus-tower scalar-scope
surfaces:

- \(F_g^{\mathrm{diag}}(\cA)=\kappa(\cA)\lambda_g^{\mathrm{FP}}\)
  is a diagonal scalar cohomology-class statement, not the full
  all-weight genus tower by default;
- the full all-weight formula requires genus one, or a uniform-weight
  lane / supplied cross-channel correction together with strict
  Mittag--Leffler completion;
- \(\delta F_g^{\mathrm{cross}}\) is the mixed-edge stable-graph
  correction and may not be silently set to zero for multi-weight
  \(W\)-families;
- analytic "free energy" or "partition function" language requires a
  separate VOA trace-convergence, analytic partition-function, and
  renormalization/SDR package;
- finite stable-graph enumeration certifies finite-window diagonal
  scalar Faber--Pandharipande coefficients only, unless the
  cross-channel and completion hypotheses are returned explicitly.

The eleventh pass repairs standard-family affine computation surfaces:

- affine Kac--Moody conductor formulas are non-critical generic-lane
  statements; \(k=-h^\vee\) is a separate Feigin--Frenkel center lane;
- scalar vanishing of \(k+h^\vee\) at the critical level is not a
  generic Koszul-conductor proof and does not make the Sugawara, KZ, or
  bar-diagonal package defined;
- conductor helpers must return status/ambient/object scope or reject
  critical examples rather than treating them as ordinary C3 boundary
  values;
- examples lacking theorem status, ambient, and object scope are
  quarantined until those three fields are supplied.

The twelfth pass repairs Virasoro exceptional-charge surfaces:

- \(\mathrm{Vir}_c^! = \mathrm{Vir}_{26-c}\) is a theorem-scoped
  duality statement, not an unqualified object equality;
- \(K^\kappa(\mathrm{Vir}_c)=13\) is the algebra-level scalar conductor
  lane and does not by itself certify the full class-\(\mathsf M\)
  shadow tower;
- \(c=0\) and \(c=-22/5\) are singular for the universal
  \(S_4=10/[c(5c+22)]\) normalization and require a separate
  quotient/renormalized-shadow calculation;
- \(c=26\) is the critical string charge with dual charge \(0\), not
  the Virasoro self-dual point;
- \(c=13\) is the Koszul self-dual fixed point.

The thirteenth pass repairs principal \(\mathcal W_N\) conductor surfaces:

- the principal \(\mathcal W_N\) strong-generator spin set is
  \(\{2,\ldots,N\}\);
- the central-charge conductor is
  \(K_c(\mathcal W_N)=4N^3-2N-2\), with first values
  \(26,100,246,488\);
- the scalar Koszul conductor is
  \(K^\kappa(\mathcal W_N)=(H_N-1)K_c(\mathcal W_N)\), so
  \(\mathcal W_3\) gives \(250/3\) and \(\mathcal W_4\) gives
  \(533/2\);
- \(K_c\) and \(K^\kappa\) are distinct lanes and may not be
  interchanged or inferred from ghost spin sums without the anomaly
  ratio \(H_N-1\).

The fourteenth pass repairs Bershadsky--Polyakov / non-principal
\(\mathcal W\)-algebra surfaces:

- \(\mathrm{BP}_k\) is the subregular/minimal
  \(\mathfrak{sl}_3\) Drinfeld--Sokolov branch
  \(\mathcal W^k(\mathfrak{sl}_3,f_{(2,1)})=\mathcal W^{(2)}_3\), not
  the principal \(\mathcal W_N\) branch;
- the strong generators are
  \(J_{h=1}^{\mathrm{bos}},G^+_{h=3/2}^{\mathrm{ferm}},
  G^-_{h=3/2}^{\mathrm{ferm}},T_{h=2}^{\mathrm{bos}}\);
- the scalar package splits into the \(J\)-line
  \((2k+3)/3\), the \(T\)-line \(c_{\mathrm{BP}}(k)/2\), the mixed
  odd pairing \((k+1)(2k+3)\), the full modular characteristic
  \(c_{\mathrm{BP}}(k)/6\), and the presentation-dependent DS ghost
  leg;
- \(c_{\mathrm{BP}}(k)=2-24(k+1)^2/(k+3)\),
  \(K_c=196\), and \(K^\kappa=98/3\);
- the orbit \((2,1)\) is self-transpose, but same-family Koszul
  duality is theorem-scoped by the subregular DS/bar transport
  package; the fixed real level \(k=-3\) is a pole, not an attained
  self-dual VOA point.

The fifteenth pass repairs \(\mathcal N=2\) superconformal-algebra
surfaces:

- the OPE package is the four-generator
  \(T,J,G^+,G^-\) package; spectral flow is an automorphism of this
  package, so it proves OPE/shadow invariance under \(\sigma_\theta\),
  not chiral Koszulness by itself;
- the total modular-Koszul characteristic is the Kazama--Suzuki/coset
  value
  \(\kappa_{\mathcal N=2}(c)=(6-c)/(2(3-c))=(k+4)/4\);
  the channel curvature sum \(c/2+c/3+c/3=7c/6\) is a diagnostic
  multi-channel sum and may not be used as the total \(\kappa\);
- the Koszul-dual central charge is the additive involution
  \(c\mapsto 6-c\), with self-dual free-field/pole point \(c=3\);
  the old \(c\mapsto 9/c\) lane is rejected for this surface;
- genus-one scalar helpers use
  \(F_1=\kappa/24=(6-c)/(48(3-c))\) and must mark \(c=3\) as an
  undefined chart value rather than assigning the channel-sum value;
- G-line termination and the full \(\mathcal N=2\) Koszulness claim
  remain conditional until the G-line quartic contact computation and
  the Kazama--Suzuki, Feigin--Frenkel transport, completed PBW/bar,
  finite-window or completed Verdier, and spectral-flow OPE-invariance
  hypotheses are returned explicitly.

The sixteenth pass repairs lattice-VOA self-duality and theta-scope
surfaces:

- the lattice input is an even, non-degenerate, positive-definite
  lattice with a normalized Borcherds-symmetric FLM cocycle; a helper
  that does not return this package is not allowed to assert the VOA,
  theta, or Koszul surface unconditionally;
- \(D(\Lambda)=\Lambda^*/\Lambda\) is the discriminant group.  For
  non-unimodular lattices the theta statement is a discriminant-form /
  vector-valued theta surface, not an implicit scalar modular-form
  assertion;
- \(\kappa(V_\Lambda)=\operatorname{rank}(\Lambda)\) and
  \(\kappa(V_\Lambda^!)=-\operatorname{rank}(\Lambda)\) are scalar
  Verdier-dual curvature statements, with complementarity sum \(0\);
- unimodularity gives bar-coalgebra self-duality
  \(V_\Lambda^i\cong V_\Lambda^c\) on the intrinsic bar-dual coalgebra
  when the inverse cocycle is cohomologous to the original one.  It
  does not assert \(V_\Lambda^!=V_\Lambda\) as algebras;
- executable lattice helpers now distinguish
  `bar_coalgebra_self_dual` from `koszul_algebra_self_dual` and return
  a typed lattice scope record carrying the even-lattice,
  discriminant, cocycle, theta, and Verdier-dual hypotheses.

The seventeenth pass repairs moonshine, K3/Mukai, and symmetric-orbifold
surfaces:

- Monster moonshine, the Leech lattice VOA, and the K3/Mukai lane are
  three different source objects.  \(V^\natural\) carries the Monster
  moonshine constants; \(V_{\mathrm{Leech}}\) carries the rank-\(24\)
  lattice constants; K3/Mukai constants are not obtained from either
  without an explicit comparison morphism, normalisation of the
  \(\kappa\)-family, source-object identification, and invariance proof.
- symmetric-orbifold twist sectors are conjugacy classes of \(S_N\),
  equivalently partitions of \(N\).  A helper that omits the partition
  surface has not defined the fixed-point sector data.
- fixed-point Koszulness for \(\operatorname{Sym}^N(X)\) is conditional
  on the seed Koszul/PBW package, a finite group action preserving the
  OPE and conformal vector, all twisted sectors, rational/C2-cofinite or
  finite-type twisted-module control, derived fixed-point or exact
  invariant comparison, the bar comparison between fixed points,
  invariant bar, and twisted sectors, and completed finite-weight /
  strict Mittag--Leffler passage.
- DMVV is used here as a character, Euler-characteristic, or
  elliptic-genus coefficient identity.  It is not a bar-complex theorem
  and does not by itself prove fixed-point Koszulness.

The eighteenth pass repairs triplet \(\mathcal W(p)\) logarithmic-VOA
surfaces:

- \(\mathcal W(p)\), \(p\ge2\), is the \(C_2\)-cofinite logarithmic
  triplet family with central charge \(1-6(p-1)^2/p\), strong
  generators \(T\) of weight \(2\) and \(W^+,W^0,W^-\) of weight
  \(2p-1\), and \(2p\) simple modules.
- \(C_2\)-cofiniteness is a proved/finiteness input, not a Koszulness
  theorem.  It also forbids free strong generation by the finite
  positive-weight generator set: a free strong generator set would leave
  a polynomial, hence infinite-dimensional, \(C_2\)-quotient.
- chiral Koszulness of \(\mathcal W(p)\) is conjectural/open on this
  surface.  Finite-window PBW agreement is evidence only; finite-window
  PBW excess detects relations but does not by itself compute the full
  bar cohomology.
- the off-Theorem-H object is the high-degree Hochschild defect complex
  \(\mathrm{KD}_{\mathrm H}^{\bullet}(\mathcal W(p))\).  Theorem H
  concentration may be claimed only after the logarithmic bar package,
  Kac--Shapovalov control, completion, and defect-vanishing hypotheses
  are returned explicitly.

The nineteenth pass repairs admissible-level simple-quotient surfaces:

- at admissible level \(k=-h^\vee+p/q\), the universal affine algebra
  \(V_k(\mathfrak g)\) and the simple quotient
  \(L_k(\mathfrak g)=V_k(\mathfrak g)/N_k\) are different objects.
  Here \(N_k\) is the maximal proper graded null-vector ideal.
- the proved universal PBW / chiral-Koszul theorem lives on
  \(V_k(\mathfrak g)\).  It does not automatically descend to
  \(L_k(\mathfrak g)\), because the bar construction is not right
  exact.
- quotient Koszulness for \(L_k(\mathfrak g)\) requires the quotient
  bar comparison package: explicit filtered null-vector ideal, a
  completed comparison morphism \(B(V_k)\to B(L_k)\), Tor/bar spectral
  sequence control, finite-weight or completed quotient comparison for
  the induced differential, and vanishing of quotient-created
  high-degree bar/Hochschild defects.
- ribbon/modular tensor structure, \(C_2\)-cofiniteness, rationality,
  associated-variety collapse, high null-vector weight, and low-weight
  character agreement are evidence or companion structure; none is a
  replacement for the quotient bar comparison.

The twentieth pass repairs super-Yangian and exceptional-Yangian RTT
surfaces:

- for \(Y_\hbar(\mathfrak{gl}_{m|n})\), the parity convention is part
  of the object: the first \(m\) basis vectors are even, the last
  \(n\) are odd, and \(|E_{ij}|=p_i+p_j\pmod 2\).
- the ordered bar differential uses total degree
  \(|x|+p_x\), and after desuspension the Koszul sign is
  \((-1)^{(|x|-1+p_x)(|y|-1+p_y)}\).
- the supertrace normalization is
  \(\operatorname{str}(E_{ij}E_{ji})=(-1)^{p_i}\).  On the
  normalized finite-window line,
  \(\kappa^{\operatorname{str}}_{m,n}(k)
    = \frac{m+n}{2}(k+m-n)\), and the Feigin--Frenkel dual level is
  \(k^!=-k-2(m-n)\).
- the Berezinian normalization used by compute is the explicit
  shifted value
  \(\kappa^{\operatorname{sBer}}=\kappa^{\operatorname{str}}
   +\frac12\max(m,n)\); any manuscript surface needing an
  independent analytic derivation of that shift from the full
  Berezinian contraction must cite that proof obligation.
- for exceptional Yangians, a spectral/Yang--Baxter check in a chosen
  finite representation window is not a full RTT presentation theorem.
  Type \(A_n\), orthogonal \(P,Q\), or generic RTT formulas do not
  extrapolate to \(G_2,F_4,E_6,E_7,E_8\).  Each exceptional window
  requires its own tensor-product decomposition, Casimir eigenvalues,
  spectral finite-window check, and a separate Drinfeld/J-presentation
  or RTT presentation with PBW/flatness control before being promoted.
- \(E_6,E_7,E_8\) Kac--Moody shadow data are computed directly from
  their dimensions and dual Coxeter numbers; they are not inherited
  from type \(A\) RTT formulas.

## Evidence Required

A surface is repaired only if current sources prove one of the
following:

- it is explicitly fixed-carrier/convolution-level and cites
  `thm:convolution-d-squared-zero`;
- it is relative log-FM ambient and carries `\ClaimStatusConditional`
  with the signed residue-pushforward package;
- it is a finite-window computation that states which part is
  coefficient-combinatorial and which part still needs geometric
  residue-pushforward comparison.
- it names the five firewall objects by type:
  \(A\), \(B_X(A)\), \(A^{\mathrm i}=H^\bullet B_X(A)\), \(A^!\), and
  \(Z_{\mathrm{ch}}^{\mathrm{der}}(A)\), and any arrow between them names
  the functor and hypothesis package;
- a Hilbert-series comparison between bar cohomology and \(A^!\) is
  explicitly a dimension comparison through finite-type or completed
  Verdier/linear duality, not an object-level equality.
- any Theorem B / exact-recovery / QEC decoding surface records:
  `applies`, `raw_direct_sum_chain_qi`, `ambient`, and the finite-window
  or completed strict-ML hypothesis package.
- any Theorem H / `ChirHoch` amplitude \([0,2]\) surface records the
  PBW chiral Koszul, finite-type/perfect, genericity,
  \(E_\infty\)-completion, strict Mittag--Leffler, and PBW/Arnold
  contraction hypotheses, or else names
  \(\mathrm{KD}_{\mathrm H}^{\bullet}(A)\) as the off-package defect
  complex.
- no compute helper may return a degree-\(\{0,1,2\}\) Hochschild vector
  without either an explicit Theorem H scope record or an explicit
  rejection of the off-Theorem-H surface.
- no K3/BKM/Delta5 compute helper may promote scalar product checks to
  \(\mathbf H_{\Delta_5}\) recognition without returning the
  four-part datum \((\beta,\delta,\varepsilon,\tau)\) and the
  finite-window Hall source/completion checks.
- no MC5 audit may demand a global `PROVED` aggregate unless it also
  names the ambient.  Valid audit records must distinguish proved
  analytic/coderived/strict-completed surfaces from the class
  \(\mathsf M\) raw direct-sum failure, the conditional tree-level
  amplitude pairing, and downstream physical comparison surfaces.
- no open/closed helper may identify
  \(Z_{\mathrm{ch}}^{\mathrm{der}}(A)\) with a physical bulk
  factorization algebra unless it returns the OCA comparison data and
  records the ambient completion in which the comparison is a
  quasi-isomorphism.
- no QEC or tensor-network helper may label bar-cobar inversion as
  physical bulk reconstruction; it may only state an algebraic analogy
  unless it returns the OCA comparison package.
- no ordered-to-symmetric helper may claim that averaging commutes with
  \(d_B\), preserves the convolution bracket, or gives a chain-level
  symmetric bar map unless it returns the \(R\)-twisted descent package
  and the missing-hypothesis list is empty.
- no Theorem C / shifted-symplectic helper may promote scalar Verdier
  sums, genus-series cross-pairings, or rank-one scalar Gram matrices
  to a C2 Lagrangian theorem unless it returns the full C2
  hypothesis package and an empty missing-hypothesis list.
- no Theorem D / genus-tower helper may promote
  \(F_g^{\mathrm{diag}}=\kappa\lambda_g^{\mathrm{FP}}\), finite
  graph sums, or formal radius-of-convergence checks to the full
  all-weight tower or analytic free energy unless it returns the
  cross-channel, strict Mittag--Leffler, and analytic hypothesis
  packages required for that stronger claim.
- no standard-family helper may treat affine critical-level scalar
  vanishing as a generic Kac--Moody conductor or duality theorem unless
  it returns the Feigin--Frenkel critical-center scope and rejects the
  Sugawara/KZ/generic conductor package.
- no Virasoro helper may call \(c=26\) self-dual, use
  \(\mathrm{Vir}_{26-c}\) as an object-level dual without the
  Virasoro duality theorem package, or apply the universal
  \(S_4=10/[c(5c+22)]\) tower at \(c=0\) or \(c=-22/5\) without a
  separate singular/renormalized-shadow scope record.
- no \(\mathcal W_N\) helper may identify the central-charge conductor
  \(K_c\) with the scalar Koszul conductor \(K^\kappa\), or leave
  \(N\geq4\) as unimplemented, when it claims the general principal
  \(\mathcal W_N\) conductor formula.
- no Bershadsky--Polyakov helper may treat \(\mathrm{BP}_k\) as a
  principal \(\mathcal W_N\) example, collapse the \(J\)-line,
  \(T\)-line, odd pairing, full \(\kappa\), and DS ghost leg into one
  scalar, or call \(k=-3\) an attained self-dual real-level point.
- no \(\mathcal N=2\) superconformal helper may use \(7c/6\) as the
  total modular-Koszul \(\kappa\), use \(c\mapsto 9/c\) as the
  Koszul-dual central-charge map, or mark G-line termination /
  \(\mathcal N=2\) Koszulness proved without returning the missing
  quartic-contact and coset/PBW/completion/transport hypothesis list.
- no lattice-VOA helper may infer \(V_\Lambda^!=V_\Lambda\) from
  unimodularity, collapse the intrinsic bar-dual coalgebra
  \(V_\Lambda^i\) into the Verdier-dual algebra \(V_\Lambda^!\), or
  assert scalar theta modularity for a non-unimodular lattice without
  returning the discriminant-form / vector-valued theta surface.
- no symmetric-orbifold helper may promote DMVV to bar-complex theorem
  status, omit the twist-sector partition data, or mark fixed-point
  Koszulness proved unless the missing fixed-point/bar comparison
  hypotheses list is empty.
- no moonshine helper may transport Monster or Leech constants into the
  K3/Mukai lane unless it returns the comparison morphism,
  normalisation, source-object identification, and invariance proof.
- no triplet \(\mathcal W(p)\) helper may report two strong generators,
  infer Koszulness from \(C_2\)-cofiniteness or finite-window PBW
  agreement, mark free strong generation as global, or omit the
  high-degree Hochschild defect object.
- no admissible-level helper may mark \(L_k(\mathfrak g)\) Koszul, or
  claim that the universal affine theorem descends, from universal PBW,
  ribbon/modular tensor structure, \(C_2\)-cofiniteness, rationality,
  high null-vector weight, associated-variety collapse, or finite
  low-weight character agreement unless the quotient bar comparison
  package is returned and its missing-hypotheses list is empty.
- no super-Yangian helper may compute a shadow or bar differential
  without returning the \(\mathbb Z/2\)-parity convention, matrix-unit
  parity rule, desuspended bar sign, and supertrace normalization.
- no exceptional-Yangian helper may promote a finite spectral/YBE
  window, type \(A\) RTT formula, or orthogonal \(P,Q\) test matrix to
  a full \(G_2,F_4,E_6,E_7,E_8\) RTT presentation unless it returns
  the type-specific presentation theorem and PBW/flatness comparison.

## Twenty-first pass: Hall--Borcherds / K3 recognition gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 701--736 and 737--744 at the
executable K3/BKM surface.

- before the five recognition gates D1--D5 are complete, the finite
  Hall--Borcherds object is labelled \(H_{\Delta_5}^{\mathrm{target}}\),
  not \(H_{\Delta_5}\);
- the name \(H_{\Delta_5}\) and the statement
  \(\Omega B(H_{\Delta_5})\simeq H_{\Delta_5}\) are unlocked only by
  the complete D1--D5 package: compact K3 Hall source and finite
  height/charge/weight window; associated-graded Hall/Borcherds
  identification; augmentation/coproduct/completion/inverse-system
  maps; parity/PBW/no-extra-root/no-central/no-torsion checks; and
  bar--cobar comparison maps preserving product, coproduct,
  differential, augmentation, averaging, finite-window counits, and
  strict Mittag--Leffler passage;
- finite K3 elliptic-genus coefficients, Borcherds product exponents,
  Weyl-vector prefactor checks, and sampled super root dimensions are
  scalar/finite-window evidence only;
- the K3 Mukai scalar \(K^\kappa=8\), the Borcherds weight
  \(\kappa_{\mathrm{BKM}}=5\), the fibre Mukai rank \(24\), the
  compact \(K3\times E\) categorical value \(0\), and the Heisenberg
  chiral value \(3\) are disjoint lanes.  No number moves between
  these lanes without a source-level comparison morphism.

## Twenty-second pass: CY-to-chiral staging and Hilb/Fock lift split

This pass repairs PDF obligations 745--756 at the executable
second-quantization surface.

- the CY-to-chiral surface is always recorded as the two-stage
  composition
  \[
    \Phi_d^{(\Sigma_{d-1},C)}
      = \Sp^{\mathrm{ch}}_{\Sigma_{d-1},C}\circ\Phi_d^{\mathrm{FA}},
  \]
  never as a bare one-stage \(\Phi_d\);
- a composition claim is conditional until the reference curve \(C\),
  the transverse manifold \(\Sigma_{d-1}\), factorization-homology
  hypotheses, and the \(HH^{-1}=0\) slice (when used) are supplied;
- the \(d=2\) surface slice and the \(d\geq3\) transverse-factorization
  slice are reported separately;
- the Hilbert-scheme/Fock bridge is a computed character/Euler/Fock
  bridge, not a categorical lift and not a bar theorem;
- the categorical lift is conjectural by default unless an explicit
  source category, functor on objects and morphisms,
  monoidal/factorization compatibility, and comparison with the
  Hilbert-scheme/Fock bridge are supplied;
- the scalar coincidence \(5=2+3\) is recorded as a numerical
  coincidence only.  It is not a BPS/chiral \(\kappa\)-sum theorem and
  does not move numbers between lanes without a comparison morphism.

## Twenty-third pass: CoHA, Hall--Drinfeld, Lusztig, and PBW scope

This pass repairs PDF obligations 757--765 at the executable
root-of-unity quantum-group surface.

- a CoHA/Hall--Drinfeld claim is conditional until the CoHA source,
  Hall product and coproduct, nondegenerate Hall pairing or radical
  quotient, Drinfeld-double completion, Lusztig root-of-unity
  specialization, finite quantum-group presentation, and PBW basis are
  all supplied;
- the existing \(u_q(\mathfrak{sl}_2)\) computation is scoped to the
  simply-connected small quantum group presentation at a primitive
  root order \(N\).  It does not by itself define a CoHA source or a
  Hall--Drinfeld double;
- the claimed \(\zeta_8,\zeta_{12},\zeta_{24}\) PBW dimensions are
  computed only on that stated presentation:
  \(8^3=512\), \(12^3=1728\), and \(24^3=13824\);
- finite admissible spectra of the modular Yangian witness
  Frobenius--Lusztig Casimir data, but do not reconstruct the full
  Frobenius--Lusztig center;
- Kazhdan--Lusztig/Verlinde evidence is not a proved bar recovery of
  the truncated quantum group until the bar collision residue functor,
  braiding preservation, fusion-product preservation, modular
  \(S\)-matrix compatibility, and root-of-unity truncation
  compatibility are supplied.

## Twenty-fourth pass: Humbert--Heegner and nearby-cycle gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 766--775 at the executable
Igusa/Fourier--Jacobi surface.

- Humbert divisors are defined with the standard discriminant filter
  \(D>0\) and \(D\equiv0,1\pmod4\); invalid discriminants are rejected,
  and \(H_4\) is explicitly flagged as a convention-sensitive label;
- finite admissible Heegner unions are accepted only when every
  discriminant passes the Humbert filter;
- the nearby-cycle theorem surface is conditional until the
  bi-unipotent Malcev ladder, codimension-\(3\) transversality theorem,
  codimension-\(4\) emptiness theorem, nearby-cycle functor
  \(\psi_{\mathrm{nw}}\), bar-filtration compatibility,
  \(\varprojlim^1\) obstruction formula, \(\phi_{-2,1}\) coefficient
  convention, and Baily--Borel compatibility are all supplied;
- the \(\phi_{-2,1}\) coefficient accessor returns the exact
  Eichler--Zagier normalization, \((n,\ell)\), discriminant
  \(D=4n-\ell^2\), and source table, so coefficient use cannot float
  without convention.

## Twenty-fifth pass: Heegner comparison and associator scope

This pass repairs PDF obligations 776--780 at the executable
\(H_{\Delta_5}\) recognition surface.

- \(H_{\Delta_5}\) is a recognition theorem, not a construction
  theorem, until both the D1--D5 finite Hall--Borcherds gates and the
  Heegner comparison gates are complete;
- the Heegner comparison gates require the Humbert/Heegner union,
  Malcev ladder plus codimension transversality/emptiness,
  nearby-cycle and bar-filtration compatibility, and
  \(\varprojlim^1\)/Baily--Borel compatibility packages;
- \(\Phi^{\mathrm{Sieg\text{-}Bor}}\) is conjectural by default.  It
  becomes constructed only when a Hall realization and an all-order
  pentagon proof are both supplied;
- if only the finite calculation through order \(\hbar^3\) is present,
  the status says exactly that: verified through \(\hbar^3\), not all
  orders;
- scalar Siegel/Borcherds target data is never called an associator on
  a Hall realization unless non-scalar source data and the all-order
  pentagon proof are present.

## Twenty-sixth pass: physical bulk/OCA and Swiss-cheese operation gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 781--794 at the executable
Swiss-cheese finite-model surface.

- the computed closed-sector dimension vector is explicitly the
  universal derived-centre slot \(Z^{\mathrm{der}}_{\mathrm{ch}}(A)\),
  not a physical bulk observable factorization algebra;
- physical-bulk or holographic language is unlocked only after the
  OCA package is supplied: \(\mathcal O^{\mathrm{phys}}_{\mathrm{bulk}}(A)\)
  is defined, the comparison map
  \[
    \mathrm{OCA}\colon
      \mathcal O^{\mathrm{phys}}_{\mathrm{bulk}}(A)
      \longrightarrow Z^{\mathrm{der}}_{\mathrm{ch}}(A)
  \]
  is defined, and the OCA map is proved a quasi-isomorphism in the
  ambient completion;
- the finite dimension model now returns a default
  `physical_bulk_oca_scope` with `derived_center_is_physical_bulk=False`
  and `holographic_language_allowed=False`;
- a full \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\) operation claim is gated by
  operation spaces, codimension-one generators, codimension-two
  relations, the closed-colour Arnold relation, the open-colour
  Stasheff relation, the mixed square relation, the no-open-to-closed
  rule, the closed-colour retract, and the derived-centre action
  proof;
- minimal generators are not asserted unless the full generator list is
  marked known;
- the ordered bar complex remains a one-coloured twisting coalgebra.
  The scope record returns `bar_complex_carries_sc_ch_top=False` even
  in the all-gates-positive test, where the positive claim is only the
  \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\) action on the derived-centre pair.

## Twenty-seventh pass: raw \(E_3^{\mathrm{top}}\) topologisation gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 795--800 at the executable
Theorem-H/\(E_3\) rectification surface.

- a cochain \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\)/brace operation package
  is no longer recorded as an automatic raw
  \(E_3^{\mathrm{top}}\) physical-bulk theorem;
- the executable gate mirrors
  `master_concordance.tex::conv:master-topologisation`: a conformal
  vector \(T\) is not enough.  The raw chain-level theorem requires
  \(G\), the identity \([Q,G]=T\), filtration/completion
  compatibility, finite propagation or an explicitly completed
  ambient, SDR-independence of transferred operations, and anomaly
  cancellation in \(H^1/H^2\);
- the engine separates the weaker BRST-cohomology upgrade from raw
  chain-level transfer: \([Q,G]=T\) plus anomaly control can certify
  an \(E_3\) statement on BRST cohomology while T3/T4 remain open;
- the forward implication
  "Koszulness \(\Rightarrow E_3^{\mathrm{top}}\)-formality" is now
  recorded as conditional on T1--T5, not automatic from
  \(E_2\)-formality or operadic homotopy-Koszulity;
- at affine critical level \(k=-h^\vee\), the gate forces
  `critical_level_failure`: the Sugawara denominator vanishes, so the
  non-critical class-\(L\) topologisation route cannot be used.  The
  remaining lane is the critical Feigin--Frenkel \(E_2\)-topological
  closed-sector surface, not the non-trivial raw \(E_3\) theorem.

## Twenty-eighth pass: finite PVA/BV/QME and boundary vertex gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 801--812 at the executable
BV/BRST rectification surface.

- a finite-type PVA now supports a classical BV action only after the
  finite PVA, BV fields/antifields, odd symplectic pairing, and action
  functional are all supplied;
- the statement "CME iff PVA Hamiltonian condition" is certified only
  after the Hamiltonian condition and field-parity signs are also
  present;
- the finite PVA/CME package never promotes to an all-loop QME.  The
  QME gate remains blocked until the analytic SDR, Stokes image choice,
  self-image renormalisation, field-parity signs, renormalization
  package, and all-loop counterterm control are supplied;
- Si Li's chiral QME/Jacobi theorem is recorded as a theorem in its
  renormalized chiral package, not as a free all-loop QME theorem for
  this engine without the analytic package above;
- the boundary vertex algebra, boundary OPE theorem, and reflected
  weight identity are separated: boundary OPEs require the vertex
  algebra plus OPE maps plus proof, while the reflected weight identity
  is `UNDEFINED`, `CONDITIONAL_PENDING_PROOF`, or `PROVED` according to
  its own definition/proof gates;
- the aggregate 801--812 scope is positive only when the finite
  PVA/CME, analytic all-loop QME, and boundary/reflected-weight gates
  are all positive at once.

## Twenty-ninth pass: Chern-Simons/HT, slab, Poisson-sigma, and AGT gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 813--824 at the executable
3d holomorphic-topological comparison surface.

- the affine Chern-Simons comparison now requires the affine
  Kac--Moody boundary algebra, the Chern-Simons action/comparison, and
  the Chern-Simons-to-current map before it is even defined;
- the abelian and nonabelian conclusions are separate proof gates:
  abelian Chern-Simons yields the Heisenberg centre only when that
  proof is supplied, and nonabelian HT Chern-Simons yields affine
  currents only when that proof is supplied;
- perturbative finiteness, the Costello--Gwilliam factorization
  algebra, and the declared classical/perturbative-quantum level are
  explicit gates, so no comparison can float between classical and
  quantum meanings;
- the 3d HT bulk factorization algebra is never identified with the
  curve-level chiral algebra: the executable scope records the latter
  as the boundary algebra/boundary shadow and the former as the
  physical HT factorization algebra;
- the \(\mathcal W_3\) slab-reduction claim is blocked until the slab
  geometry, slab boundary conditions, pushforward to the curve,
  \(\mathcal W_3\) PVA, DS/BRST map, lambda-bracket match, and anomaly
  control are all present;
- the Poisson sigma model lane now separates definition of the PSM
  fields/target/action/boundary conditions from the stronger HT
  enhancement theorem, which also needs a factorization algebra and a
  proof;
- AGT is `EXTERNAL_MOTIVATION_ONLY` by default.  It becomes theorem
  language only after the parameter dictionary, Nekrasov side,
  conformal-block side, operator-algebra map, and equality/equivalence
  proof are all supplied.

## Thirtieth pass: line-operator DK, Baxter, and quantum-group convention gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 825--838 at the executable DK-0
evaluation-module comparison surface.

- the line-operator category is not treated as implicit: it is a gate
  separate from the definition of evaluation modules;
- evaluation modules generate the line-operator category only after the
  generation proof and thick-generation hypotheses are supplied;
- MC3 is certified only on the evaluation-generated core.  The full DK
  boundary is explicitly `open`, and the executable scope never permits
  a full-DK-boundary theorem from the evaluation-core gate;
- the Baxter retraction is a type-\(A\) construction: it is available
  on `sl*` lanes and is explicitly blocked outside type \(A\);
- the quantum-group parameter is gated by the convention
  \(q=\exp(\pi i/(k+h^\vee))\), not by a floating symbol \(q\);
- KZ monodromy signs, modular \(T\)-matrix conventions,
  self-monodromy vs mutual monodromy, the framing square root, and all
  conversion proofs are separate convention gates;
- the executable convention scope records that KZ monodromy is not the
  braiding and self-monodromy is not mutual monodromy;
- the DK-0 test surface now skips only the SciPy-specific ODE
  cross-checks when SciPy is absent; the analytic, numerical, quantum
  Casimir, Yangian, Verlinde, and Hecke paths still run.

## Thirty-first pass: physics, entropy, celestial, and holographic-tuple gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 839--850 at the executable Front-F
physics horizon surface.

- theorem names are gated as algebraic objects first: physics terms do
  not become theorem names, and physical language can enter only as a
  separated corollary after the algebraic theorem statement exists;
- entropy formulas are gated through character asymptotics.  A
  character-asymptotic entropy statement can be recorded before the
  BTZ theorem, but BTZ entropy theorem language remains blocked until
  modular invariance, a large-\(n\) regime, and the proof are supplied;
- celestial comparison no longer follows from shared OPE notation.  It
  requires the celestial comparison, celestial algebra input,
  factorization comparison map, comparison proof, and theorem scope;
- the old unqualified AdS/CFT payload in `physics_horizon.py` has
  been replaced by a conditional algebraic bar-cobar comparison
  requiring a seven-object tuple with maps;
- holographic reconstruction is gated by a seven-object tuple, maps
  among the entries, removal of unsupported AdS/CFT identifications, a
  reconstruction proof, and explicit failure modes when the maps are
  absent;
- the aggregate Front-F scope remains blocked unless the theorem-name,
  entropy, celestial, and holographic-tuple gate families all pass at
  once.

## Thirty-second pass: arithmetic shadow, Hecke/CPS, and Dirichlet gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 851--870 at the executable arithmetic
rectification surface.

- the arithmetic shadow tower is no longer implicit: the source
  \(\Theta_A\), the functor out of \(\Theta_A\), the moment
  \(L\)-function, the Rankin--Selberg integral, and its convergence
  domain are separate gates;
- meromorphic continuation is allowed only when either it is not
  claimed or the continuation proof is supplied;
- the Hecke action on \(\mathcal M_{1,1}\) and its lift to
  \(\mathfrak g_A^{\mathrm{mod}}\) are separate gates, so a modular
  Hecke correspondence does not automatically act on the modular
  convolution algebra;
- prime-locality is gated as a precise conjecture/theorem.  The
  lattice VOA case requires a proof whenever it is claimed, while the
  non-lattice case is explicitly a named hypothesis;
- CPS hypotheses, the representation \(\pi_r\), and the
  \(\mathrm{GL}(2)\to\mathrm{GL}(r+1)\) functoriality hypothesis for
  \(r\ge5\) are required before scoped Ramanujan comparison language
  can be promoted;
- unconditional Ramanujan claims remain blocked; the unconditional
  theorem slot is the Kim--Sarnak bound where that is the available
  theorem;
- Hecke--Newton closure is defined separately from its lattice
  finite-Hecke-span proof.  Non-lattice and irrational extensions are
  never theorem lanes in this gate; the irrational extension must be
  explicitly conditional;
- Dirichlet \(L\)-functions arising from the shadow metric are a
  definition gate, not inherited from the divisor-sum computations.

## Thirty-third pass: spectral, Borcherds/Igusa, bracket, and spine gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 871--900 at the executable arithmetic
rectification surface.

- spectral decomposition is gated by a proved decomposition, a defined
  Roelcke--Selberg basis, and a proof of compatibility with the chiral
  partition function;
- the sewing operator and sewing--Selberg formula are separate gates,
  so the Rankin--Selberg computation does not by itself define the
  operator whose determinant is being integrated;
- the Saito--Kurokawa lift, the known-scope genus-two bridge, and the
  BĂ¶cherer bridge are separate gates.  Critical-line access is theorem
  language only when proved; otherwise it can only be marked
  conditional;
- \(\Delta_5\), \(c_\Delta(0)\), and
  \(\kappa_{\mathrm{BKM}}=c(0)/2\) are gated in order.  The CHL scope
  is explicitly restricted to \(N\in\{1,2,3,4,6\}\), and CHL constants
  never transfer automatically to the K3 Mukai \(K^\kappa\);
- \(\Phi_{10}\), any associator-cocycle appearance, any
  \(\eta^{24}\) quotient, modular weights, transformation laws,
  Fricke LDP data, sub-leading corrections, and
  Shimura--Waldspurger conversion are all independent gates;
- the Shimura--Waldspurger lane requires the conversion definition, the
  weights \(k+1\in\{7,9,11\}\), and either a proof or a precise theorem
  citation;
- the Yetter--Drinfeld/Schauenburg bracket and all claimed
  \(\delta(n)\) values are gated before use.  Arithmetic brackets may
  not be mixed with the bar differential without a comparison map;
- a GRT action on K3--BKM is gated by definition; transitivity is a
  theorem only when proved and otherwise must be marked conjectural;
- arithmetic consequences are kept beyond the theorem spine unless a
  needed algebraic implication is proved.

## Thirty-fourth pass: theorem-title, theorem-signature, and proof-obligation gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 901--932 at the executable
concordance rectification surface.

- theorem titles are gated against informal adjectives: "Platonic" is
  forbidden in theorem titles and allowed only in informal remarks;
- conjectures must sit in numbered conjecture environments, and
  conditional theorem surfaces must place hypotheses before
  conclusions;
- a theorem title containing conditional language is blocked unless
  the title's hypotheses are complete;
- every theorem statement is gated by the full type signature:
  raw/finite/completed, ordered/symmetric, chain/derived/coderived,
  \(E_1/E_\infty/\mathsf{SC}/E_3\), curve-genus scope,
  critical-level exclusions, genericity exclusions, finite-type,
  completion, dualizability, holonomicity, and base-change hypotheses;
- every proof opening is gated by the ambient category, differential,
  filtration, and spectral sequence when a spectral sequence is used;
- proof methods are guarded by use-sensitive obligations:
  convergence cites the convergence theorem; inverse limits kill
  \(\lim^1\); duality checks finite/continuous duality; Verdier
  duality checks holonomicity; Gysin checks orientation; pushforward
  checks properness; \(\Sigma_n\)-quotients check equivariance;
  \(1/n!\) states characteristic zero; \(R\)-matrix descent states
  \(R\)-twisted equivariance; PBW states associated graded; and
  Koszulness states diagonal concentration.

## Thirty-fifth pass: advanced proof-method and table-status gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 933--949 at the executable
concordance rectification surface.

- formality claims are gated by the specific model and obstruction
  groups; \(A_\infty\) transfer is gated by SDR data;
- modular-operad arguments require the graph convention, stable-graph
  arguments define legs/edges/genus, sign arguments cite the
  determinant-line convention, and ghost arguments define the BRST
  complex;
- central-charge arguments define the convention, \(\kappa\)-arguments
  define the trace map, \(K^\kappa\) arguments prove \(A^!\) exists,
  \(K^c\) arguments prove the central charge of \(A^!\), and
  \(K^{\mathrm{ghost}}\) arguments state presentation dependence;
- OPE tables are blocked unless full coefficients are provided and
  matched to a normalization appendix;
- every table entry must cite the theorem or proposition proving it;
- a `proved` table status requires a manuscript proof, a `conditional`
  table status lists exact conditions, and an `open` table status names
  the obstruction complex.

## Thirty-sixth pass: structure, dependency-language, Morita, and quadrant gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 950--980 at the executable
concordance rectification surface.

- duplicate theorem statements, repeated sign appendices, and repeated
  five-object-firewall remarks are gated into merged surfaces, with the
  firewall early and cross-referenced everywhere;
- motivational physics, unproved cross-volume claims, K3 recognition
  targets, arithmetic consequences, and examples are placed after the
  algebraic theorem spine in their correct lanes;
- the verification order is executable: Heisenberg first, affine
  Kac--Moody second, \(\beta\gamma\) third, Virasoro/\(\mathcal W_3\)
  as the class-\(\mathbf M\) completion test, and \(H_\Delta\) only
  after class-\(\mathbf M\) completion;
- dependency graph arrows are gated as proved implications only;
  conjectural arrows are removed;
- comparison-theorem language is gated: "therefore" is replaced by
  "under hypotheses"; "universal" requires a universal property; and
  "canonical" requires uniqueness or contractibility of choices;
- chosen-vacuum data, vacuum-independence claims, the level-0 open
  factorization category, and Morita equivalence to the module category
  are all separate gates;
- Morita equivalence is never treated as algebra isomorphism;
- the level alphabet is defined once, level signatures are exhaustive
  only in the Open quadrant, and level signatures cannot transfer CY
  claims;
- the quadrant grid and cross-quadrant maps are gated: preservation of
  structures must be proved when claimed, and conjectural maps must be
  marked conjectural.

## Thirty-seventh pass: notation, hypothesis-index, abstract, and final-diagram gates

This pass repairs PDF obligations 981--1000 at the executable
concordance rectification surface.

- the notation table is gated before the main theorem, unused symbols
  are removed after definition, and the overloaded letters \(C\),
  \(D\), \(d\), and \(\Delta\) are separated by role;
- \(D\) is reserved for Verdier duality, \(d\) for differentials, and
  diagonal/coproduct/discriminant uses of \(\Delta\) must carry
  distinguishing subscripts;
- \(FM/FM^{\log}/FM^{\mathrm{ord}}\), bar notation,
  \(CH^{\mathrm{ch}}/HH^{\mathrm{alg}}/THH\), and
  \(Z^{\mathrm{der}}_{\mathrm{ch}}(A)/Z(A)/Z_{\mathrm{Dr}}\) are
  gated as distinct notation lanes;
- the hypothesis index for \(H1\)--\(H4\), \(CP1\)--\(CP3\),
  \(D1\)--\(D5\), \(FH\), and \(OCA\) must exist before those
  packages are referenced;
- missing section references are blocked, and every "standard
  landscape" invocation must point to a defined finite list;
- landscape coverage is theorem language only when proved; otherwise
  the manuscript surface must use atlas language;
- the arXiv abstract is constrained to the theorem spine, while
  conjectural physics/arithmetic may appear only as labelled final
  abstract material;
- the first twenty pages are gated to prove type-correctness of the
  core definitions, and the last theorem is gated as the commutative
  diagram of exactly the surviving invariants.

## Thirty-eighth pass: introduction finite-atlas repair

This pass moves obligation 995--996 from gate language into the
opening manuscript surface.

- the introduction now defines the standard landscape, at first use,
  as the finite atlas of Heisenberg, affine Kac--Moody,
  \(\beta\gamma\), Virasoro/principal \(\mathcal W\), and finite-rank
  even-lattice charts, with genericity and completion hypotheses
  supplied by the theorem using the chart;
- the previous sentence saying that the higher-genus bar complex
  "classifies" the standard families was replaced by the precise
  statement that the ordered bar complex assigns Koszul,
  shadow-depth, and modular-residue invariants to each chart;
- the introduction now explicitly says that this invariant assignment
  does not classify arbitrary chiral algebras.
- the Part IV and Part V openings in `main.tex` now say "finite
  standard-landscape atlas" and "stratification axis"; they no longer
  claim that the \(5{\times}5\) matrix classifies arbitrary chart
  algebras.

## Thirty-ninth pass: B-row shadow-depth and recognition-gate repair

This pass repairs a manuscript-level conflict exposed by obligations
5, 995, and 996.

- the introduction no longer says that the
  \(\mathbf H_{\Delta_5}\) comparison target has
  \(r_{\max}=\infty\) as its Vol~I shadow-depth coordinate;
- the B-row now carries \(r_{\max}=5\) after the Hall/CoHA
  source-recognition gates, while the infinite Borcherds root tower of
  the \(\Delta_5\) denominator is explicitly separated from the
  shadow-depth coordinate;

  \(r_{\max}\in\{2,3,4,\infty,\infty,5\}\) for
  \(\mathsf G/\mathsf L/\mathsf C/\mathsf M/
  \mathsf M^{\mathrm{ext}}/\mathsf B\), instead of giving the B-row
  infinite shadow depth;
- the Master Reconstruction theorem now states the finite-atlas
  \(\kappa\)-stratification as Open rows plus the CY-specialisation
  row \(\mathsf B\), with the K3\(\times E\) anchor transported to
  Vol~I only through the recognition gates.

- `theorem_universal_chiral_genus_extension_engine.py` now exposes
  `virasoro_raw_direct_sum_obstruction(N)`, the finite-mode witness
  \[
  \xi_N=\sum_{\lvert k\rvert\le N}s^{-1}L_{-k}\otimes s^{-1}L_k .
  \]
  Each finite stage belongs to the raw direct sum, but the supports
  grow as \(2N+1\); the coordinatewise limit is therefore a product /
  weight-completed pro-conilpotent element, not a raw direct-sum
  vector.
- The class-\(\mathsf M\) branch of
  `theorem_b_inversion_surface` now returns this witness as
  `raw_failure_witness`, so `raw_direct_sum_chain_qi=False` is backed
  by a concrete finite-support obstruction rather than a bare status
  flag.

  checks the \(\xi_N\) support growth, the absence of a raw direct-sum

  witness inside the class-\(\mathsf M\) ambient remark of the

## Fifty-first pass: simple-pole ChirHoch\(^1\) dimension firewall

This pass resolves the Theorem~H dimension-census drift left by the
fiftieth pass.  On the curve-level chiral-product surface,
\(\ChirHoch^1(\beta\gamma_\lambda)=
\ChirHoch^1(bc_\lambda)=0\), and the free-fermion simple-pole entry
also has \(\ChirHoch^1=0\).  Charge or ghost-number rescaling is a
zero-mode gauge direction, while the \(\lambda\)-line changes the
chosen conformal vector and the class-C scalar/contact shadow.  It is
not a degree-\(1\) chiral Hochschild tangent.

- `chiral_hochschild_engine.py` now separates curve-level
  `Der(A)/Inn(A)` from `parameter_tangents`.  The \(\beta\gamma\),

  conformal-weight and bilinear-rescaling motions remain recorded as
  non-\(\ChirHoch^1\) metadata.

  `chirhoch_dimension_engine.py`: the affected Poincare vectors are
  \([1,0,1]\), not \([1,2,1]\) or \([1,1,1]\).
- `chiral_hochschild_koszul.tex` now states the simple-pole firewall
  in the derivation-type table and formal-moduli proposition.  Class
  \(\mathsf C\) retains its quartic shadow depth, but that depth is
  explicitly a level-\(5\) scalar/contact invariant rather than a
  \(\ChirHoch^1\) tangent.
- `free_fields.tex` now gives the explicit Theorem~H row
  \((\mathbb C,0,\mathbb C)\) for both \(\beta\gamma_\lambda\) and
  \(bc_\lambda\), and separates the spin/conformal-weight line from
  the curve-level chiral product.
- Independent verification paths used in this pass: the explicit
  Clifford/simple-pole computation in
  `chiral_hochschild_koszul.tex`, the existing
  `chirhoch_dimension_engine.py` census, and the Koszul-duality row
  pairing \(bc\) with \(\beta\gamma\).

aliases on proposition or theorem environments, so the prefix is not an
epistemic status.

## Fifty-third pass: Hochschild crosswalk status firewall

This pass repairs the only current-source `ProvedHere` block found to
lean on a genuinely weaker theorem-status dependency rather than on an
untagged remark or equation.  The appendix crosswalk for Hochschild
terminology was mathematically right in spirit, but its proved
proposition contained two non-proved comparison packages: the
conditional Theorem~H amplitude statement and the conjectural
spectrum-level bar-to-\(\THH\) lift.  The repair separates the
definitional crosswalk from those packages.

- `appendices/hochschild_conventions.tex` keeps
  `prop:hochschild-crosswalk` as `\ClaimStatusProvedHere`, but its
  content is now only the type discipline:
  \(\ChirHoch\) is curve-level chiral Hochschild cohomology,
  \(\THH\) is the \(S^1\)-equivariant trace of an \(E_1\)-ring
  spectrum, \(\HHcat\) is categorical Hochschild cohomology, and
  \(\HHalg\) is the compact-generator algebra model.
- The Theorem~H amplitude clause is now the separate conditional
  remark `rem:hochschild-crosswalk-theorem-h-package`, explicitly
  importing the PBW, perfectness, genericity, \(E_\infty\)-completion,
  and strict Mittag--Leffler package of
  `thm:main-koszul-hoch`, with off-surface high-degree terms measured
  by \(\mathrm{KD}_{\mathrm H}^{\bullet}(\cA)\).
- The spectrum-level rational-shadow language is now the separate
  conjectural remark `rem:hochschild-crosswalk-spectrum-lift-package`,
  governed by `conj:spectrum-bar-lift` and the trace constraints of
  `rem:spectrum-bar-lift-trace-constraints`.  It is no longer an axiom
  of the proved crosswalk.
- Generated metadata was rebuilt with `python3 scripts/generate_metadata.py`.
  The generator now records \(4154\) tagged claims, with the two new
  appendix remarks counted as one conditional and one conjectural
  surface.  The `prop:hochschild-crosswalk` metadata now has five
  references and no longer records the stale
  `rem:spectrum-bar-lift-evidence` dependency.
- Verification run: the current-source suspicious-dependency scanner
  dropped from \(42\) to \(41\) `ProvedHere` blocks with weaker or
  untyped dependencies, removing `prop:hochschild-crosswalk` from the
  list.  `compute/tests/test_generate_metadata_parser.py` passed
  \(5/5\), and `git diff --check` passed on the touched manuscript and
  generated metadata surfaces.
- A follow-up audit checked the red-team feynman item:
  `prop:disk-local-binary-ternary-reduction` is currently conditional,
  while `prop:compactified-ternary-two-channel` is a proved residue
  theorem on \(\overline{M}_{0,4}\cong\bP^1\) under explicit
  logarithmic-form hypotheses.  No feynman edit was needed in this
  pass.

## Fifty-fourth pass: original-complex topologisation obstruction criterion

This pass repairs the class-\(\mathsf L\) topologisation dependency
surface in `en_koszul_duality.tex`.  The proved affine
Kac--Moody original-complex \(\Ethree^{\mathrm{top}}\) statements were
citing an untyped remark, even though the remark carries the precise
obstruction equation separating cohomological topologisation from a
chain-level theorem on the chosen BRST complex.  The repair makes that
criterion a proved status surface and separates the class-\(\mathsf M\)
frontier from it.

- `rem:topologization-chain-vs-cohomology` is now
  `\ClaimStatusProvedHere` with the title
  "Original-complex topologization obstruction criterion."  It records
  the proved inputs: chain-level
  \(\mathsf{SC}^{\mathrm{ch,top}}\), strict chiral Gerstenhaber brace
  structure, the Sugawara antighost contraction, cohomological local
  constancy, and Dunn additivity.
- The load-bearing equation is now explicitly a criterion:
  a chain-level original-complex lift requires an
  \(A_\infty\)-coherent degree-\((-1)\) family
  \(G=(G_1,G_2,\ldots)\) with
  \([m,G]=\partial_z\) in the brace deformation complex.  In degree
  \(n\) this is the displayed Stasheff derivation-homotopy equation;
  the obstruction after a partial solution through degree \(N\) is a
  degree-\(N+1\) cocycle in the same deformation complex.
- The class-\(\mathsf M\) sentence is no longer inside the proved
  criterion.  It is isolated as
  `rem:class-M-topologization-boundary` with
  `\ClaimStatusConjectured`, referencing the separate
  `conj:coderived-e3` programme.  Thus class \(\mathsf M\) no longer
  shadows the proved class-\(\mathsf L\) criterion.
- The illustrative conditional \(V_k(\mathfrak{sl}_2)\) Gerstenhaber
  restriction was removed from the proved criterion because it is not
  needed for the obstruction equation and would make the criterion
  depend on a conditional example.
- Generated metadata was rebuilt with `python3 scripts/generate_metadata.py`.
  The generator now records \(4156\) tagged claims:
  \(1748\) `ProvedHere`, \(337\) `Conjectured`, \(1620\)
  `Conditional`, \(420\) `ProvedElsewhere`, \(31\) `Heuristic`.
  Metadata records `rem:topologization-chain-vs-cohomology` as proved,
  `rem:class-M-topologization-boundary` as conjectured, and keeps both
  `prop:sugawara-gauge-rectification` and
  `prop:khan-zeng-topological` proved with only proved/typed inputs
  for the topologisation criterion.
- Verification run: the current-source weak-dependency scanner dropped
  from \(41\) to \(39\) `ProvedHere` blocks with weak or untyped
  dependencies, removing the class-\(\mathsf L\) topologisation

## Fifty-eighth pass: Serre--Langlands reduction status surface

This pass repairs the arithmetic Ramanujan bridge around
`rem:mc-ramanujan-bridge`.  The proved bridge cited an untyped
`rem:serre-reduction`, even though that remark carries the external
automorphic implication separating the algebraic MC/Newton data from
the analytic symmetric-power input.

- `rem:mc-ramanujan-bridge` remains `\ClaimStatusProvedHere`: it proves
  only the algebraic bridge from prime-local MC recursion and Newton
  relations to symmetric-power Dirichlet coefficient data, followed by
  a named external reduction.
- `rem:serre-reduction` is now the status-bearing
  `\ClaimStatusProvedElsewhere` surface
  `The Serre--Langlands reduction`.  It states the implication on
  normalized Satake parameters
  \(\widetilde\alpha_p,\widetilde\beta_p\): automorphy of all
  symmetric-power lifts in the class where the Luo--Rudnick--Sarnak
  local bound applies forces
  \(|\widetilde\alpha_p|=|\widetilde\beta_p|=1\), hence Ramanujan.
- The proof surface now names the exact estimate used:
  the largest normalized Satake parameter of
  \(\operatorname{Sym}^r f\) has size
  \(|\widetilde\alpha_p|^r\), while the
  Luo--Rudnick--Sarnak bound on \(\mathrm{GL}_{r+1}\) gives
  \(p^{1/2-1/((r+1)^2+1)}\); letting \(r\to\infty\) forces
  \(|\widetilde\alpha_p|\leq1\), and the product-one relation gives
  equality after interchanging the two Satake roots.
- `bibliography/references.tex` now carries the missing anchors
  `Serre1968Abelian`, `Langlands1970Problems`, and
  `LuoRudnickSarnak1999`; the remark also cites
  `NewtonThorne2021` and `Deligne1974` for the holomorphic
  algebraic-weight lane.
- Generated metadata was rebuilt with `python3 scripts/generate_metadata.py`.
  The generator now records \(4159\) tagged claims:
  \(1748\) `ProvedHere`, \(421\) `ProvedElsewhere`, \(337\)
  `Conjectured`, \(31\) `Heuristic`, and \(1622\) `Conditional`.
  Metadata records `rem:mc-ramanujan-bridge` depending on
  `prop:shadow-symmetric-power` and the now-typed
  `rem:serre-reduction`; the untyped claimish-dependency queue drops
  from \(282\) to \(281\).
- Verification run: `compute/tests/test_generate_metadata_parser.py`
  passed \(5/5\); the known weak-dependency scanner reports \(0\)
  `ProvedHere` blocks depending on known conditional, conjectural,
  heuristic, or open claims; `git diff --check` passed on the touched
  manuscript, bibliography, generated metadata, theorem index, and
  obligations ledger surfaces.

  convention of `def:kappa-scalar-vs-mumford`: normalized Heisenberg
  gives \(\kappa(\cH_1)=1\); the universal affine
  \(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_2\) level-\(1\) vacuum gives
  \[
  \kappa(V_1(\mathfrak{sl}_2))
  =\frac{\dim(\mathfrak{sl}_2)(1+h^\vee)}{2h^\vee}
  =\frac{3(1+2)}4=\frac94;
  \]
  the simple Frenkel--Kac--Segal lattice quotient is explicitly named
  as a separate lattice row; the \(E_8\) and \(D_{16}^+\) lattice rows
  use the oscillator-rank values \(8\) and \(16\); and
  \(V^\natural\) uses the Virasoro scalar lane
  \(\kappa=24/2=12\) because its weight-one Heisenberg channel is
  absent.

## Seventy-first pass: Brown--Deligne MZV dimension surface

This pass repairs
`thm:YD-delta-7-8-9 -> rem:nc-brown-deligne` and corrects a
mathematical inconsistency exposed by that dependency.

- `rem:nc-brown-deligne` in
  `chapters/theory/nilpotent_completion.tex` is now explicitly
  `\ClaimStatusProvedElsewhere`.  Its Brown motivic MZV dimension
  table was corrected to the recurrence
  \(d_n=d_{n-2}+d_{n-3}\), \((d_0,d_1,d_2)=(1,0,1)\), giving
  \[
  d_7,\ldots,d_{12}=(3,4,5,7,9,12).
  \]
  The shifted values previously printed for weights \(5\)--\(10\)
  were false in this convention.
- The proof of `thm:YD-delta-7-8-9` no longer lists a dubious
  explicit weight-\(10\) basis.  It uses Brown's dimension theorem
  equivalently as the coefficient of \(x^{10}\) in
  \((1-x^2-x^3)^{-1}\), giving \(d_{10}=7\).
- Independent checks in this session:
  direct recurrence computation gives
  \([d_7,\ldots,d_{12}]=[3,4,5,7,9,12]\); formal expansion of
  \((1-x^2-x^3)^{-1}\) gives coefficients
  \([1,0,1,1,1,2,2,3,4,5,7,9,12]\) through weight~\(12\);
  the theorem's Catalan product at \(n=10\) is then
  \(C_9d_{10}=4862\cdot7=34034\).
- Generated metadata was rebuilt with
  `python3 scripts/generate_metadata.py`.  The generator now records
  \(4293\) tagged claims: \(1814\) `ProvedHere`, \(434\)
  `ProvedElsewhere`, \(348\) `Conjectured`, \(31\) `Heuristic`,
  \(1652\) `Conditional`, \(1\) `Open`, and \(13\)
  `Definitional`.

  passed \(7/7\); the known weak-dependency scanner reports \(0\)

## Stop condition after pass 183: W17 Borcherds recognition cross-volume conflict

The next queue head,
`thm:walgdeep-gaiotto-siegel-weight -> rem:walgdeep-W17-borcherds-kN-computation`,
is not a harmless missing tag.

- In `chapters/examples/w_algebras_deep.tex`,
  `thm:walgdeep-gaiotto-siegel-weight` is marked
  `\ClaimStatusProvedHere` and states, for \(N \geq 2\), the
  class-\(\mathcal S\) constant coefficient
  \(f^{(N)}(0,0)=2(N+3)\) and the associated Borcherds/Siegel weight
  ladder.
- The theorem proof cites the Vol.~II phantom anchors
  `V2-sec:wa-supplement-iii` and `V2-prop:wa-f-constant`.
- In `~/chiral-bar-cobar-vol2/chapters/examples/w-algebras.tex`,
  `prop:wa-f-constant` is explicitly
  `\ClaimStatusConditional`: for \(N\ge 3\), \(\phi^{(N)}\) is a
  conditional symbol until finite Jacobi/Borcherds recognition is
  performed, and the displayed values \(f^{(3)}=12\),
  \(f^{(4)}=14\), \(f^{(5)}=16\) are recorded as conditional
  comparison objects, not proved Fourier coefficients.
- The adjacent Vol.~II theorem `thm:wa-siegel-weight-kN` is also
  `\ClaimStatusConditional` and says that constant coefficient alone
  does not prove existence, divisor, character, Siegel modularity, or a
  spin-cover square-root form.
- Therefore the Vol.~I proved-here theorem currently leans on a
  cross-volume conditional recognition fixture. The local W17 remark
  verifies only the \(N=3,4\) constant-term input as written; typing it
  as `ProvedHere` would not repair the general \(N\ge 2\) theorem
  surface and would mask the cross-volume status disagreement.

Per the cross-volume conflict rule, this surface should not be silently
reconciled. The principal decision is whether Vol.~I's theorem is
canonical and Vol.~II should be upgraded with the missing recognition
proof, or whether Vol.~I should be demoted/split into a proved \(N=2\)
and small-rank computation lane plus a conditional \(N\ge 3\)
Borcherds-recognition theorem.

## Three-hundred-sixty-second pass: Koszulness meta-theorem count honesty

This pass removes the remaining active surfaces that counted
Theorem~`thm:koszul-equivalences-meta` as ten unconditional
equivalences, nine unconditional compute rows, or twelve mutually
equivalent conditions. The canonical count is now the exact split
\[
7 + 1 + 2 + 1 + 1 = 12:
\]
seven independent bidirectional equivalences
\((i)--(v),(ix),(x)\), one Barr--Beck--Lurie consequence of
\((v)\), two conditional rows \((vii)\) and \((xi)\), one one-way
ChirHoch consequence \((viii)\), and one one-directional
\(\mathcal D\)-module purity implication \((xii)\).

- In Vol~I manuscript and standalone surfaces
  `chapters/frame/preface.tex`,
  `chapters/frame/preface_sections5_9_draft.tex`,
  `standalone/programme_summary.tex`,
  `standalone/programme_summary_sections2_4.tex`,
  `standalone/introduction_full_survey.tex`,
  `standalone/survey_track_a_compressed.tex`,
  `standalone/survey_modular_koszul_duality.tex`, and
  `standalone/survey_modular_koszul_duality_v2.tex`, stale
  "twelve equivalent", "ten unconditional", and "eight independent"
  formulations were replaced by the exact status split. The status
  tables now list item~\((vii)\) as conditional rather than as an
  independent genus-zero equivalence.
- In compute-facing status surfaces
  `compute/lib/theorem_koszul_12fold_rectification_engine.py`,
  `compute/lib/theorem_concordance_rectification_engine.py`,
  `compute/lib/factorization_homology_engine.py`,
  `compute/lib/theorem_pentagon_koszul_engine.py`,
  `compute/lib/holographic_code_engine.py`,
  `compute/lib/c2_cofiniteness_koszul_bridge_engine.py`, and
  `compute/lib/koszulness_ten_verifier.py`, together with their
  touched tests, the machine-readable count now separates independent
  equivalences, listed consequences, conditional comparisons, one-way
  consequences, and one-directional implications. The K11 helper in the
  twelvefold rectification engine now reports "perfectness input
  verified" while keeping `k11_unconditional` false.
- In Vol~II
  `/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar-vol2/chapters/connections/bar-cobar-review.tex`,
  `/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar-vol2/chapters/connections/concordance.tex`,

## Three-hundred-sixty-fourth pass: Strict convolution \(D^2\) proof surface

This pass closes comprehensive-cache entry~209 for

`ProvedHere`, but the old three-line proof left implicit that the Hom

model rather than in the ordered \(E_1\) or ambient log-FM models.

- In `chapters/theory/higher_genus_modular_koszul.tex`, the theorem now
  states \(D=D_{\mathrm{st}}\).  The proof computes explicitly, for a
  homogeneous
  \[
  \varphi\colon C_*(\overline{\mathcal M}_{g,n})
  \to \operatorname{End}_{\cA}(n),
  \]
  that
  \[
  D^2\varphi
  =
  d_{\operatorname{End}}^{\,2}\varphi
  -
  \varphi\partial_{\mathcal M}^{\,2}
  =0,
  \]
  with the Koszul middle terms cancelling.  The proof separates
  \(d_{\mathrm{int}}+[\tau,-]\) from the coefficient differential and
  \(d_{\mathrm{sew}}+\hbar\Delta\) from stable-curve boundary faces,
  and explicitly excludes ordered \(E_1\) curvature, planted forests,
  and relative-family curvature from this theorem.

## Three-hundred-sixty-fifth pass: Multi-channel depth-gap obstruction

This pass closes comprehensive-cache entry~208 for
Proposition~`prop:depth-gap-trichotomy`.  The single-line Riccati and
MC-recursion arguments already ruled out finite depth
\(d_{\mathrm{alg}}\geq3\) on every \(\kappa\neq0\) primary line, but
the standard-landscape theorem still needed a named obstruction
excluding a multi-channel stratum-separation pattern that would
terminate strictly beyond the contact row.

- In `chapters/theory/higher_genus_modular_koszul.tex`, a new proved
  proposition `prop:no-finite-depth-beyond-contact` states the finite
  support alternative for the standard landscape.  Decoupled sectors
  compose by the maximum of the sectorwise finite depths; the
  \(\beta\gamma_\lambda/bc_\lambda\) contact sector has
  \(\Defcyc^{(2q)}=0\) by rank-one rigidity and terminates at
  \(d_{\mathrm{alg}}=2\); and any coupled sector activates a
  non-nilpotent cubic pump and has infinite algebraic depth.  Hence no
  finite \(d_{\mathrm{alg}}\geq3\) can be assembled by multi-channel
  interaction.
- The proof of `prop:depth-gap-trichotomy` now cites this proposition
  for the multi-generator closure and no longer self-cites
  `prop:depth-gap-trichotomy` in the class-\(\mathbf C\) contact
  witness.
- In `compute/lib/depth_separation_complete.py`,
  `no_finite_depth_beyond_contact_witness()` records the same support
  alternatives and verifies that the complete standard-family table has
  finite algebraic depths exactly \([0,1,2]\), with coupled sectors
  represented by infinite depth.  The corresponding focused test was
  added to `compute/tests/test_depth_separation_complete.py`.
- In `notes/first_principles_cache_comprehensive.md`, entry~208 is
  marked resolved by this pass and points to the new manuscript and

This pass closes comprehensive-cache entry~207 for

  realization \(\iota_r^{\mathrm{oc}}(T)\), and its closed shadow
  projection \(\pi_r^{\mathrm{sh}}(T)\), and states the exact
  degreewise detection condition
  \[
  \iota_r^{\mathrm{oc}}(T)=0 \Longleftrightarrow T=0
  \Longleftrightarrow \pi_r^{\mathrm{sh}}(T)=0
  \]
  on the standard primitive support.
- Proposition~`prop:sc-formal-iff-class-g` now assumes that package
  explicitly.  Its proof cites the lemma in both directions, so
  class-\(\mathbf G\) no longer becomes SC-formal by an unnamed
  no-kernel assertion, and SC-formality no longer forces
  \(S_r=0\) through bare averaging.

  \(\kappa\)" rationale.

  uses

  \lambda_2^{\mathrm{FP}}
  =

  =
  \frac{7}{5760},

  while the GRR/\(\hat A\) route extracts the same coefficient from
  \((x/2)/\sin(x/2)-1\).  The computation explicitly separates this
  free-energy coefficient from the genus-\(2\) socle integral
  \(\int_{\overline{\cM}_2}\lambda_2\lambda_1=1/5760\).

  from "two independent proof paths" to "two comparison routes, not
  disjoint at the scalar bridge."
- In `compute/lib/faber_pandharipande_cross_verification.py`,
  `genus2_heisenberg_fp_grr_disjoint_check()` records the exact FP and
  GRR coefficients, the rank-one Heisenberg \(\kappa=1\), the resulting
  \(F_2\), and the distinct \(1/5760\) socle integral.

## Three-hundred-sixty-ninth pass: Miura triangularity under the spectral coproduct

This pass closes comprehensive-cache entry~204.  The proof of Miura
cross-term universality used the sentence "\(\Delta_z\) does not raise
\(W\)-spin" as a load-bearing Step~3 assertion, while the compute
engine encoded the same conclusion directly in its lower-sector support
model.

- In `chapters/theory/ordered_associative_chiral_kd.tex`, the new lemma
  `lem:miura-triangularity-under-Delta` is marked `\ClaimStatusProvedHere`.
  It states the type signature explicitly: Open quadrant, ordered
  associative chiral/Yangian presentation, Beilinson level \(4\to5\)
  operator-to-coproduct lane, under the generic-\(\Psi\) package
  consisting of the Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak triangular Miura basis and
  Drinfeld spectral coproduct.  The proof derives preservation of the
  largest-primary \(W\)-spin filtration from Drinfeld \(\psi\)-index
  bounds and the triangular inverse.
- The proof of `thm:miura-cross-universality-monograph` now separates the
  spin-\(2\) base case, handled by `lem:coprod-T-miura`, from the
  spin-uniform \(s\ge3\) argument.  Step~3 now cites
  `lem:miura-triangularity-under-Delta` instead of asserting
  non-raising informally.  The triangularity attribution remark now
  separates the imported PR triangular basis from the coproduct-filtration
  consequence proved here.
- In `compute/lib/miura_universality_proof_engine.py`,
  `delta_w_spin_filtration_pairs`,
  `triangular_delta_bound_for_composite`, and

  \(W\)-spin bound from Drinfeld \(\psi\)-index support and triangular
  inversion.  The legacy support model now uses that derived bound rather
  than a bare `w_value = w_spin` assignment.
- In `compute/tests/test_miura_universality_proof_engine.py`,
  `test_miura_triangularity_under_delta_finite_witness_spins_4_to_6` is

## Three-hundred-seventieth pass: DS coproduct finite window without shared-formula tautology

This pass closes comprehensive-cache entry~203.  The old DS-coproduct
intertwining evidence compared `delta_psi_sl3` with `delta_psi_w1inf`;
both functions implemented the same universal Drinfeld binomial formula,
so the advertised intertwining evidence was a shared-code convention
check, not an independent computation.

- In `chapters/theory/ordered_associative_chiral_kd.tex`, the new
  computation `comp:ds-w3-degree2-rtt-miura-witness` is marked
  `\ClaimStatusProvedHere`.  It is explicitly finite-window: Open
  quadrant, ordered associative chiral/Yangian presentation, Beilinson
  level \(4\to5\), generic \(\Psi\), principal DS projection for
  \(\mathfrak{sl}_3\), RTT coproduct, and the two-boson Miura stress
  tensor
  \(T_M={:}\psi_1\psi_2{:}-(\psi_1+\psi_2)^2/(2\Psi)\).
- The computation proves the \(z^0\), degree-\(2\)
  Cartan/Sugawara window:
  \[
  (\pi_3\otimes\pi_3)\Delta^{RTT}_{z,0}(T_M)
  -T_M\otimes1-1\otimes T_M
  =
  \frac{\Psi-1}{\Psi}(x\otimes y+y\otimes x)
  -\frac1{\Psi}(x\otimes x+y\otimes y).
  \]
  The RTT route lists and kills the six off-diagonal root terms; the
  Miura route expands primitive two-boson currents.
- Remark~`rem:ds-intertwining-w3` no longer asserts that the full
  chain-level DS coproduct identity has been proved by degree-\(1\)
  tests.  It now says degree \(1\) is tautological, the finite
  degree-\(2\) window is proved by the new computation, and the spin-\(3\)
  DS-HPL coproduct identity remains the load-bearing obligation for the
  full compatibility theorem.
- In `compute/lib/ds_coproduct_intertwining_engine.py`,
  `miura_primitive_stress_tensor_coproduct`,
  `rtt_projected_stress_tensor_coproduct`, and
  `ds_w3_degree2_rtt_miura_witness` implement the two independent
  routes.  The older `delta_T_from_psi` helper now returns the primitive
  two-boson \(z^0\) window instead of mixing the \(W_{1+\infty}\)
  generator \(\psi_2\) with the two Miura currents.
- In `compute/tests/test_ds_coproduct_intertwining_engine.py`,
  the decorated independent-verification test is now
  `test_ds_w3_degree2_rtt_miura_hz_iv`, registered against
  `comp:ds-w3-degree2-rtt-miura-witness`.  It compares projected RTT
  terms to the primitive Miura expansion and does not call
  `delta_psi_sl3` or `delta_psi_w1inf`.  The old degree-\(1\) and
  `delta_psi` equality tests remain undecorated sanity checks.
- In `notes/first_principles_cache_comprehensive.md`, entry~203 is now
  marked resolved with the finite-window scope and the remaining spin-\(3\)
  obligation named.
- Verification before metadata regeneration: the focused DS-coproduct
  test file passed \(65/65\), and the engine witness reports
  `comp:ds-w3-degree2-rtt-miura-witness`, `intertwines=True`, with six
  killed off-diagonal RTT terms.
